  // Set session ID in sessionStorage for events to pick up on and publish
  function sessionStorageGet(key) {
    try {
      if (!window.sessionStorage) return false;
  
      var encoded = window.sessionStorage.getItem(key);
      return encoded != null ? JSON.parse(encoded) : encoded;
    } catch (err) {
      if (window.Bugsnag)
        Bugsnag.notifyException(new Error("LocalStorageError"), {
          msg: "retrieving key: " + key,
          error: err,
        });
      return false;
    }
  }
  
  function sessionStorageSet(key, value) {
    var str;
  
    try {
      if (!window.sessionStorage) return;
  
      str = JSON.stringify(value);
      window.sessionStorage.setItem(key, str);
  
      return true;
    } catch (err) {
      if (window.Bugsnag)
        Bugsnag.notifyException(new Error("LocalStorageError"), {
          msg: "setting key: " + key,
          error: err,
        });
      return false;
    }
  }
  
  if(!sessionStorageGet('tr_sess_id')) {
    var timestamp = new Date().getTime().toString();
    var uid = pie.browser.getCookie("uid") || "unknown-guid";
    sessionStorageSet('tr_sess_id', uid + "_" + timestamp );
  }
